***cherubijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijn</a> (65645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cherubyn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cherubin</i>, reanalyzed as singular, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cherubin</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cherubim</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χερουβίμ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kheroubím</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblical_Hebrew" class="extiw" title="w:Biblical Hebrew">Biblical Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">כְּרוּבִים</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k'ruvím</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> originally plural.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijnen.html>cherubijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cherub</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">angel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lamassu-like angel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> six-winged humanoid angel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">putto</span></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cherub</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">affectionate term for a child</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">all angelic senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">cherub</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:cherubijn.html>cherubijn</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(Jiddisch-Hebreeuws)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:engel.html>engel</a></li></ol>
</body>

***chipper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a> (94616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From English dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nimble; frisky</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of obscure origin. Perhaps akin to Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kjapt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">briskly; impetuously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kippa</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"to snatch; pull; jerk" gt; Middle English <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kipra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wrinkle; draw tightly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Norwegian <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">kjapp</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fast; brisk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize; catch; <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kip.html>kip</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Exhibiting a lively optimism; in high <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a>, cheerful.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> April 29,  Nathan Rabin,  “TV: Review: THE SIMPSONS (CLASSIC): “Treehouse of Horror III” (season 4, episode 5; originally aired 10/29/1992)”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.avclub.com/articles/treehouse-of-horror-iii,72723/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The idea of a merchant selling both <a href = vnd.unilang:totems.html>totems</a> of pure evil and frozen yogurt (he calls it frogurt!) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> amusing in itself, as <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the idea that frogurt could be cursed, but it’s really the Shopkeeper’s <a href = vnd.unilang:quicksilver.html>quicksilver</a> shift from ominous doomsaying to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chipper.html>chipper</a></b> salesmanship that sells the sequence.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fish and chip shop, or more generally a cheap fast food outlet, typically selling <a href = vnd.unilang:chips.html>chips</a> and other deep-fried foods.</li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chlore</i>, formed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chlorine</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphry_Davy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Humphry Davy">Humphry Davy</a> based on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χλωρός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khlōrós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cho.html>cho</a> (13678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kweman</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">chuman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwemaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kommen.html>kommen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">come</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">koma</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌵𐌹𐌼𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qiman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formazza" class="extiw" title="w:Formazza">Formazza</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> Realp <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canton_of_Uri" class="extiw" title="w:Canton of Uri">Uri</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come</li></ol>

***chocolade.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chocolade.html>chocolade</a> (3688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">chocolate</i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nahuatl" class="extiw" title="w:Nahuatl">Nahuatl</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> word, though it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not clear precisely which one. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chocolate</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Chocolate.jpg/250px-Chocolate.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="195" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Chocolate.jpg/375px-Chocolate.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Chocolate.jpg/500px-Chocolate.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="934" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:chocolade.html>Chocolade</a></i><br />Chocolate</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chocolade.html>chocolade</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>chocolate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the past some dictionaries prescribed a feminine gender, likely because of analogy with <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> that have the ending <i>-ade</i>. This prescription does not seem to have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> any basis in common usage or etymology, however.
</p>

***chop-chop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chop-chop.html>chop-chop</a> (84332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_Pidgin_English" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese Pidgin English">Chinese Pidgin English</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">速速</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cuk1 cuk1</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chop-chop.html>chop-chop</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Used to urge someone to do something quickly</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chop-chop.html>chop-chop</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Quickly.
<ul><li><b>1977</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Le_Carr%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Le Carré">John Le Carré</a>, <i>The Honourable Schoolboy</i>, Folio Society 2010, p. 13:
<dl><dd>‘And another <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>! But <i>cold</i> this time, hear that, boy? <i>Muchee coldee</i>, and bring it <i><b>chop chop</b></i>.’</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chop-chop.html>chop-chop</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tobacco that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> produced and <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> without excise (tax), and therefore cheap and illegal.
<ul><li><b>1944</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australian_House_of_Representatives" class="extiw" title="w:Australian House of Representatives">Australian House of Representatives</a>, <i>Parliamentary Debates</i>, Volume 265, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=BpMqAQAAIAAJamp;q=%22chop-chop%22+tobacco+-intitle:%22chop-chop%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;dq=%22chop-chop%22+tobacco+-intitle:%22chop-chop%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=xj0lT7_3NaKQiQeX27T2BAamp;redir_esc=y">page 30968</a>,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> are here today to try and do the impossible: to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> the <b>chop chop</b> industry.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2002</b> November 11, <i>Major ‘<b>chop chop</b>’ seizure in Northern Queensland</i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australian_Taxation_Office" class="extiw" title="w:Australian Taxation Office">Australian Taxation Office</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160310022549/https://www.ato.gov.au/corporate/content.asp?doc=%2Fcontent%2Fmr2002106.htm">media release</a>.</li>
<li><b>2007</b>, Martin Hughes, <i>The Slow Guide: Melbourne</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=XWnN1XKjRTkCamp;pg=PT95amp;dq=%22chop-chop%22+tobacco+-intitle:%22chop-chop%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=2j8lT8LbOc7trQebkoS4CAamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22chop-chop%22%20tobacco%20-intitle%3A%22chop-chop%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">unnumbered page</a>,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:attitudes.html>Attitudes</a> to tobacco mean it′s virtually <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> under the counter (and we′re not talking about ‘<b>chop chop</b>’).</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***choqueren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:choqueren.html>choqueren</a> (52202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">choquer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:choqueren.html>choqueren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike (e.g. with poverty)</li></ol>

***chorizo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chorizo.html>chorizo</a> (57873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:chorizo.html>chorizo</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chorizo.html>chorizo</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chorizos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A spicy Spanish sausage flavoured with <a href = vnd.unilang:paprika.html>paprika</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b> January–February,  Mark Bittman,  “The only 7 meals you need for 2008”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Men%27s_Health" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Men | s Health"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a>'s Health</a></cite>, volume 23, number 1, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/1054-4836">1054-4836</a></small>, page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=6ccDAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA138amp;dq=%22chorizo%22">138</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Substitute three chopped scallions and a minced jalapeño for the onion, and 6 ounces crumbled <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chorizo.html>chorizo</a></b> for the tomatoes. Sub ½ cup <a href = vnd.unilang:queso.html>queso</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fresco.html>fresco</a> for the <a href = vnd.unilang:parmesan.html>Parmesan</a> in step 2. Serve with salsa.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***chow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a> (17692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow-chow.html>chow-chow</a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_Pidgin_English" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese Pidgin English">Chinese Pidgin English</a> of unclear origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Food, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:snacks.html>snacks</a>.
<dl><dd><i>I'm going to pick up some <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></b> for dinner.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>Chow</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>Chow</a>.
<ul><li><b>1914</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saki" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Saki"><a href = vnd.unilang:saki.html>Saki</a></a>, ‘The Lull’, <i>Beasts and Superbeasts</i>:
<dl><dd>‘I'd try and grapple with him myself, only I've got my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></b> in my room, you know, and he goes for pigs wherever he finds them.’</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1988</b> March 4,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> Weinberg,  “First Person: <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>Me</a> and Georgia <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Keeffe”, in  <cite>Chicago Reader</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://securesite.chireader.com/cgi-bin/Archive/abridged2.bat?path=1988/880304/OKEEFFE">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">While <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> talking, one of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>, the <a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a> one, <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> come <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> and I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> absently petting him.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> now  <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A Chinese person.
<ul><li><b>1938</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xavier_Herbert" class="extiw" title="w:Xavier Herbert">Xavier Herbert</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Capricornia_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Capricornia (novel)">Capricornia</a></i>, Chapter V, p. 74, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/capricornianovel00herb">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>These <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:creatures.html>creatures</a> Nawnim <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> amazed to see about him on the day of his arrival. When he inquired about them, <a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> him they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> Japs an' <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>Chows</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1977</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Le_Carr%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Le Carré">John Le Carré</a>, <i>The Honourable Schoolboy</i>, Folio Society 2010, p. 11:
<dl><dd>‘Now look here old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> if you should ever bump into an interesting <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>Chow</a></b> from <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the river – one with <i>access</i>, follow <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>? – just you remember High <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>Haven</a>!’</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">chowing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">chowed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/South_Africa" class="extiw" title="w:South Africa">South Africa</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To eat.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">州</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zhōu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A prefecture or district of the second rank in China, or the chief city of such a district.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phono-semantic_matching" class="extiw" title="w:Phono-semantic matching">Phono-semantic matching</a> of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">吃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chī</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to eat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by the “food” sense of Etymology 1 above.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:mahjong.html>mahjong</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A run of three consecutive tiles of the same suit.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">chowing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">chowed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:mahjong.html>mahjong</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To call a discarded tile to produce a <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Eleanor Noss Whitney,  <cite>A Mah <a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>Jong</a> Handbook: How to Play, Score, and Win</cite>, page 154:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> while the adversary on his right will repeatedly bury in the discard the very tiles he wishes to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></b> but can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***christen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a> (6556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cristen</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kersten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Christiānus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Χρῑστιᾱνός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Khrīstiānós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The current Dutch spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> influenced by the Latin and subsequently also the Greek <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christenen.html>christenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">christin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Christian</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerstijndom</i>, with the first element <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> modified to agree with the Latin/Greek spelling. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-dom</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:christenen.html>christenen</a> (7579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christenen.html>christenen</a></strong>
